### .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: CI

on:
  push:
  pull_request:

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Set up Python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.11"

      - name: Install deps
        run: |
          python -m pip install --upgrade pip
          if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then pip install -r requirements.txt; fi
          if [ -f requirements-dev.txt ]; then pip install -r requirements-dev.txt; fi
          pip install pytest

      - name: Run tests
        run: pytest -q

### v2/validate.py
from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import asdict, is_dataclass
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Tuple


def _to_obj(x: Any) -> Any:
    if is_dataclass(x):
        return asdict(x)
    return x


_ALLOWED_ACTIONS = {
    "NOOP",
    "OPEN_LINK_INDEX",
    "WEB_LOOKUP_QUERY",
    "SUGGESTION_ACCEPT",
    "SUGGESTION_REJECT",
    "SUGGESTION_DEFER",
    "SUGGESTION_REVISE",
    "PROPOSED_ACTION_COMMIT",
    "SPOTIFY_COMMAND",
    "STATE_SET_AWAKE",
    "ENTER_TASK_INTAKE",
    "TIME_READ",
    "PRIORITY_GET",
    "PRIORITY_SET",
}


def validate_engine_output(obj: Any) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
    o = _to_obj(obj)
    if not isinstance(o, dict):
        return False, "EngineOutput must be a dict-like object"

    required = ["route_kind", "speak_text", "actions", "state_delta", "mode_set", "followup_until_utc", "debug"]
    for k in required:
        if k not in o:
            return False, f"missing field: {k}"

    if not isinstance(o["route_kind"], str) or not o["route_kind"].strip():
        return False, "route_kind must be non-empty string"

    if not isinstance(o["speak_text"], str):
        return False, "speak_text must be string"

    if not isinstance(o["actions"], list):
        return False, "actions must be list"

    for i, a in enumerate(o["actions"]):
        if not isinstance(a, dict):
            return False, f"actions[{i}] must be dict"
        if "type" not in a or "payload" not in a:
            return False, f"actions[{i}] must include type and payload"
        if not isinstance(a["type"], str) or not a["type"].strip():
            return False, f"actions[{i}].type must be non-empty string"
        if not isinstance(a["payload"], dict):
            return False, f"actions[{i}].payload must be dict"

        t = a["type"]
        if t not in _ALLOWED_ACTIONS:
            return False, f"actions[{i}].type not allowed: {t!r}"

        p = a["payload"]

        if t == "OPEN_LINK_INDEX":
            if "target" not in p:
                return False, "OPEN_LINK_INDEX payload must include target"
            tgt = p.get("target", None)
            if tgt is not None and not isinstance(tgt, (int, str)):
                return False, "OPEN_LINK_INDEX target must be int, str, or None"

        if t == "WEB_LOOKUP_QUERY":
            q = p.get("query", None)
            if not isinstance(q, str) or not q.strip():
                return False, "WEB_LOOKUP_QUERY query must be non-empty string"


        if t == "SUGGESTION_ACCEPT":
            sid = p.get("suggestion_id", None)
            if not isinstance(sid, str) or not sid.strip():
                return False, "SUGGESTION_ACCEPT suggestion_id must be non-empty string"

        if t == "PROPOSED_ACTION_COMMIT":
            pid = p.get("proposal_id", None)
            if not isinstance(pid, str) or not pid.strip():
                return False, "PROPOSED_ACTION_COMMIT proposal_id must be non-empty string"
            return True, ""

        if t == "SPOTIFY_COMMAND":
            cmd = p.get("cmd", None)
            if not isinstance(cmd, str) or not cmd.strip():
                return False, "SPOTIFY_COMMAND cmd must be non-empty string"
            q = p.get("query", None)
            if q is not None and not isinstance(q, str):
                return False, "SPOTIFY_COMMAND query must be string or None"

        if t == "STATE_SET_AWAKE":
            if "awake" not in p or not isinstance(p.get("awake"), bool):
                return False, "STATE_SET_AWAKE awake must be bool"


        if t == "TIME_READ":
            # Read-only: payload may be empty dict
            pass

        if t == "PRIORITY_GET":
            # Read-only: payload may be empty dict
            pass

        if t == "PRIORITY_SET":
            # State change: allow item/priority to be present or omitted; payload must be dict (already enforced)
            item = p.get("item", None)
            pr = p.get("priority", None)
            if item is not None and not isinstance(item, (str, int)):
                return False, "PRIORITY_SET item must be str, int, or None"
            if pr is not None and not isinstance(pr, (str, int)):
                return False, "PRIORITY_SET priority must be str, int, or None"
        if t == "ENTER_TASK_INTAKE":
            if "enabled" not in p or not isinstance(p.get("enabled"), bool):
                return False, "ENTER_TASK_INTAKE enabled must be bool"

    if not isinstance(o["state_delta"], dict):
        return False, "state_delta must be dict"

    if o["mode_set"] not in ["IDLE", "INTAKE", "FOLLOWUP_OPEN", "FOLLOWUP_SCHEDULE"]:
        return False, "mode_set invalid"

    if o["followup_until_utc"] is not None and not isinstance(o["followup_until_utc"], str):
        return False, "followup_until_utc must be None or string"

    if not isinstance(o["debug"], dict):
        return False, "debug must be dict"

    return True, ""



def validate_named(name: str, obj: Any) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
    if name == "EngineOutput":
        return validate_engine_output(obj)
    return False, f"unsupported validation target: {name}"


### v2/engine_adapter.py
from __future__ import annotations


def _normalize_web_query(raw: str) -> str:
    """
    WEB_QUERY_NORMALIZE_V1
    Deterministic, rules-only normalization for web lookup queries.
    Goal: turn messy transcripts into stable search queries without guessing.
    """
    q = (raw or "").strip()

    # Drop a leading "hey vera," if it survived upstream
    q = re.sub(r"^\s*hey\s+vera\s*,?\s*", "", q, flags=re.I)

    # Remove common intent prefixes
    q = re.sub(r"^\s*(search\s+(the\s+)?web\s+(for\s+)?)", "", q, flags=re.I)
    q = re.sub(r"^\s*(web\s*search\s+(for\s+)?)", "", q, flags=re.I)
    q = re.sub(r"^\s*(look\s*up\s+)", "", q, flags=re.I)
    q = re.sub(r"^\s*(lookup\s+)", "", q, flags=re.I)
    q = re.sub(r"^\s*(google\s+)", "", q, flags=re.I)
    q = re.sub(r"^\s*(find\s+)", "", q, flags=re.I)
    q = re.sub(r"^\s*(search\s+for\s+)", "", q, flags=re.I)

    # Normalize whitespace + punctuation edges
    q = q.replace("—", "-").replace("–", "-")
    q = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", q).strip(" \t\r\n.,!?;:")

    # --- Numeric normalization (targeted) ---
    # 9-11 / 9 11 / nine eleven -> 911 (ONLY in a context where it's likely a model number)
    q_low = q.lower()

    has_911_signal = bool(
        re.search(r"\b9\s*[- ]\s*11\b", q_low) or
        re.search(r"\b911\b", q_low) or
        re.search(r"\bnine\s+eleven\b", q_low)
    )

    if has_911_signal:
        q = re.sub(r"\b9\s*[- ]\s*11\b", "911", q, flags=re.I)
        q = re.sub(r"\bnine\s+eleven\b", "911", q, flags=re.I)

    # --- Transcript-noise correction (HIGH PRECISION only) ---
    # Only rewrite "portion/portia/porchia" -> "porsche" when 911 signal is present.
    if has_911_signal:
        q = re.sub(r"\bportion\b", "porsche", q, flags=re.I)
        q = re.sub(r"\bportia\b", "porsche", q, flags=re.I)
        q = re.sub(r"\bporchia\b", "porsche", q, flags=re.I)
        q = re.sub(r"\bporche\b", "porsche", q, flags=re.I)

    # Final cleanup
    q = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", q).strip()
    return q

import time
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from v2.state_reducer import reduce_pds
from v2.validate import validate_named

import re


def _normalize_web_search(raw: str) -> Dict[str, str]:
    """
    Deterministic v2-only normalization.
    Returns:
      {"mode": "PASS", "raw": raw}
      {"mode": "FOLLOWUP", "speak": "..."}
    """
    s = (raw or "").strip()
    low = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s.lower()).strip()

    # Bare intent: requires a follow-up (no actions)
    if low in {"search the web", "search web", "search the internet", "search internet", "web search"}:
        return {"mode": "FOLLOWUP", "speak": "What would you like me to search the web for?"}

    # Normalize common phrases to a v1-friendly pattern that yields WEB_LOOKUP
    patterns = [
        r"^(search the web for)\s+(.+)$",
        r"^(search for)\s+(.+)$",
        r"^(look up)\s+(.+)$",
        r"^(lookup)\s+(.+)$",
        r"^(find)\s+(.+)$",
    ]
    for pat in patterns:
        m = re.match(pat, s.strip(), flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        if m:
            q = (m.group(2) or "").strip()
            if q:
                # v1 already supports "look up X"
                return {"mode": "DIRECT_WEB_LOOKUP", "query": q}

    return {"mode": "PASS", "raw": s}


def _normalize_context_v1(ctx: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    CONTEXT_V1 (non-binding)
    Deterministic normalization:
    - None / non-dict -> {}
    - allowlist keys only (matches schema additionalProperties:false)
    - coerce values to strings (stable JSON surface)
    """
    if not isinstance(ctx, dict):
        return {}
    allowed = ("active_app", "local_date", "local_time", "screen_hint")
    out: Dict[str, Any] = {}
    for k in allowed:
        v = ctx.get(k, None)
        if v is None:
            continue
        out[k] = str(v)
    return out



@dataclass(frozen=True)
class EngineInput:
    raw_text: str
    wake_required: bool = True
    priority_enabled: bool = True
    awake: bool = True
    timestamp_utc: Optional[str] = None
    context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    pds: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class EngineOutput:
    route_kind: str
    speak_text: str
    actions: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    state_delta: Dict[str, Any]
    mode_set: str
    followup_until_utc: Optional[str]
    debug: Dict[str, Any]


    context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
def _error_output(code: str, detail: str) -> EngineOutput:
    out = EngineOutput(
        route_kind=code,
        speak_text="",
        actions=[{"type": "NOOP", "payload": {"error": detail}}],
        state_delta={},
        mode_set="IDLE",
        followup_until_utc=None,
        debug={"error": detail},
    )
    ok, _ = validate_named("EngineOutput", out)
    if ok:
        return out
    return out


def run_engine_via_v1(inp: EngineInput) -> EngineOutput:
    raw = (inp.raw_text or "").strip()


    # === M11W1_COMMIT_GATE ===
    # Deterministic, v2-only commit gate (proposal-only).
    # - Never executes anything.
    # - Emits explicit metadata action only when operator says: "commit <proposal_id>"
    m = re.match(r"^\s*commit\s+([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{3,64})\s*$", raw, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
    if m:
        pid = m.group(1)
        out = EngineOutput(
            route_kind="PROPOSED_ACTION_COMMIT",
            speak_text="",
            actions=[{"type": "PROPOSED_ACTION_COMMIT", "payload": {"proposal_id": pid}}],
            state_delta={"awake": bool(inp.awake), "mode": "IDLE"},
            mode_set="IDLE",
            followup_until_utc=None,
            debug={"normalized": True, "commit": True, "proposal_id": pid},
            context=_normalize_context_v1(inp.context),
        )
        ok, err = validate_named("EngineOutput", out)
        if not ok:
            return _error_output("ERROR_SCHEMA_OUTPUT", err)
        return out

    # === M9W3_ACCEPT_SUGGESTION ===
    # Deterministic, v2-only acceptance loop.
    # - Never executes anything.
    # - Emits an explicit action only when operator says: "accept <suggestion_id>"
    # === M10W1_REVIEW_CONTROLS ===
    # Deterministic, v2-only review controls.
    # - Never executes anything.
    # - Never generates proposals.
    # - Emits explicit metadata actions only.
    m = re.match(r"^\s*reject\s+([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{3,64})\s*$", raw, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
    if m:
        sid = m.group(1)
        out = EngineOutput(
            speak_text="",
            state_delta={"awake": bool(inp.awake), "mode": "IDLE"},
            mode_set="IDLE",
            followup_until_utc=None,
            route_kind="SUGGESTION_REJECT",
            actions=[{"type": "SUGGESTION_REJECT", "payload": {"suggestion_id": sid}}],
            debug={"normalized": True, "review": True, "verb": "reject", "suggestion_id": sid},
            context=_normalize_context_v1(inp.context),
        )
        ok, _ = validate_named("EngineOutput", out)
        return out

    m = re.match(r"^\s*defer\s+([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{3,64})\s*$", raw, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
    if m:
        sid = m.group(1)
        out = EngineOutput(
            speak_text="",
            state_delta={"awake": bool(inp.awake), "mode": "IDLE"},
            mode_set="IDLE",
            followup_until_utc=None,
            route_kind="SUGGESTION_DEFER",
            actions=[{"type": "SUGGESTION_DEFER", "payload": {"suggestion_id": sid}}],
            debug={"normalized": True, "review": True, "verb": "defer", "suggestion_id": sid},
            context=_normalize_context_v1(inp.context),
        )

./GLOSSARY.md:25:- allow-for-commit
./GLOSSARY.md:29:### Commit
./GLOSSARY.md:30:An explicit, attributable, synchronous operator authorization that allows execution.
./GLOSSARY.md:31:A commit is the only mechanism that can transition from decision to execution.
./GLOSSARY.md:34:- commits cannot be inferred
./GLOSSARY.md:35:- commits cannot be delegated to the system
./GLOSSARY.md:36:- commits do not grant permanent authorization
./GLOSSARY.md:40:Execution must never occur without a valid commit.
./GLOSSARY.md:42:### Receipt
./GLOSSARY.md:43:An auditable record of what the system decided and what happened.
./GLOSSARY.md:44:Receipts are required for accountability.
./GLOSSARY.md:50:### Refusal
./GLOSSARY.md:52:Refusals are first-class outcomes and not errors.
./GLOSSARY.md:55:A refusal due to missing permission or missing authority.
./GLOSSARY.md:56:In this repo, denials are typically represented as refusal outcomes with authority-related reason codes.
./GLOSSARY.md:68:## Governance terms
./GLOSSARY.md:71:A non-negotiable constraint that defines what the system will not do.
./GLOSSARY.md:75:A stable identifier for why a refusal or constraint triggered.
./GLOSSARY.md:79:An append-only record of proposals, decisions, commits, and outcomes.
./GLOSSARY.md:84:- what the system claims
./GLOSSARY.md:85:- what it actually does
./GLOSSARY.md:86:- what was authorized
./GLOSSARY.md:91:A time-to-live boundary that prevents stale context from being reused to justify action.
./GLOSSARY.md:98:### Hat
./GLOSSARY.md:99:A domain governance lens that applies domain-specific constraints without changing core engine semantics.
./GLOSSARY.md:100:A hat adds rules and classifications, not power.
./GLOSSARY.md:102:### Coat
./GLOSSARY.md:103:A presentation layer that maps stable reasons and outcomes to human-readable messages.
./GLOSSARY.md:104:A coat may improve legibility, but must not change meaning.
./GLOSSARY.md:114:### Prefer refusal over unsafe action
./GLOSSARY.md:115:Ambiguity is resolved by refusal or failure, not execution.

./docs/refusal_model.md:1:# Refusal Model (Taxonomy v1)
./docs/refusal_model.md:4:Refusals preserve user control, prevent unsafe action, and maintain deterministic boundaries.
./docs/refusal_model.md:5:A refusal is a correct outcome, not an error.
./docs/refusal_model.md:8:- refusal vs failure vs denial vs unavailability
./docs/refusal_model.md:9:- refusal categories (exhaustive)
./docs/refusal_model.md:11:- required refusal fields
./docs/refusal_model.md:12:- examples that survive adversarial review
./docs/refusal_model.md:18:### Refusal
./docs/refusal_model.md:19:A deliberate, deterministic “no” based on invariants, scope, authority, safety, or expired context.
./docs/refusal_model.md:26:A hard “not permitted” due to authority/permission constraints (e.g., missing explicit commit, missing platform permission).
./docs/refusal_model.md:32:- If it is a policy/invariant/authority decision → REFUSAL or DENIAL
./docs/refusal_model.md:38:## Required refusal fields (every refusal must include)
./docs/refusal_model.md:39:A refusal response must include these fields in the ledger (and must be representable in any UI without changing meaning):
./docs/refusal_model.md:45:- `actionability`: what the user can do next (or "none")
./docs/refusal_model.md:46:- `commit_required`: true/false (true only when explicit user commit would resolve it)
./docs/refusal_model.md:47:- `risk_note`: short phrase describing what risk is being prevented (no speculation)
./docs/refusal_model.md:58:## Refusal categories (exhaustive)
./docs/refusal_model.md:61:Refusal because explicit authority was not provided or cannot be inferred.
./docs/refusal_model.md:62:Typical: missing commit, ambiguous intent, attempted delegation.
./docs/refusal_model.md:65:Refusal because the request is out of declared capability bounds or violates explicit chat/project scope (e.g., UI work out of scope).
./docs/refusal_model.md:68:Refusal because the request increases power or weakens determinism, auditability, or consent alignment.
./docs/refusal_model.md:71:Refusal because the request violates a locked invariant (see `docs/invariants.md`).
./docs/refusal_model.md:74:Refusal because required context is expired or stale and cannot be used to justify action.
./docs/refusal_model.md:77:- Denials are represented as REFUSAL with category AUTHORITY and a DENY_* reason code.
./docs/refusal_model.md:78:- Unavailability is not a refusal category; it is reported as UNAVAILABLE outcomes elsewhere, but may be surfaced as SCOPE when a capability is explicitly excluded.
./docs/refusal_model.md:85:- AUTH_NO_COMMIT
./docs/refusal_model.md:86:  - No explicit commit provided for an authority-requiring action.
./docs/refusal_model.md:90:  - The request attempts to delegate commit/authority to the system.
./docs/refusal_model.md:93:- DENY_COMMIT_DISALLOWED
./docs/refusal_model.md:94:  - Commit requested but disallowed by invariants or scope.
./docs/refusal_model.md:108:  - Adds ambiguity, heuristics, or non-deterministic behavior.
./docs/refusal_model.md:109:- SAFE_BLURS_PROPOSAL_COMMIT
./docs/refusal_model.md:110:  - Collapses proposal/decision/commit boundaries.
./docs/refusal_model.md:134:  - Request references prior approvals/state that cannot be reused.
./docs/refusal_model.md:141:Refusal messages must be legible and consistent. The system may vary tone, but must preserve meaning.
./docs/refusal_model.md:144:  - “I can’t proceed without an explicit commit from you.”
./docs/refusal_model.md:146:  - “That request is out of scope for this track.”
./docs/refusal_model.md:160:| “Do that automatically next time.” | SCOPE | SCOPE_AUTONOMY_OUT_OF_SCOPE | Autonomy is out of scope and disallowed. | None |
./docs/refusal_model.md:161:| “Just go ahead and commit it for me.” | AUTHORITY | AUTH_DELEGATION_ATTEMPT | Commit cannot be delegated to the system. | Provide explicit commit yourself |
./docs/refusal_model.md:164:| “Skip the refusal logs to keep it clean.” | SAFETY | SAFE_UNAUDITABLE_ACTION | Removing audit logs weakens accountability. | None |
./docs/refusal_model.md:165:| “Add a UI overlay for refusals.” | SCOPE | SCOPE_UI_OUT_OF_SCOPE | UI work is explicitly out of scope. | None |

./docs/refusal_model.md:172:- Collapse “proposal vs commit”
./docs/refusal_model.md:174:- Retry automatically after refusal

./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:1:# REMOVAL SAFETY (HATS + COATS)
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:7:- Hat: governance layer that may interpret or explain within its scope, but never executes and never escalates authority.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:8:- Coat: explanation-only layer that maps reason codes to language; it never decides.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:12:### Coat Removal (Explanation Layer)
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:13:Removing a coat MUST:
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:15:- not change any refusal/allow result
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:20:Allowed effect of coat removal:
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:26:- if removing a coat changes what happens (not just what is said), the system is invalid.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:28:### Hat Removal (Governance Interpretation Layer)
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:29:Removing a hat MUST:
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:33:- not bypass refusal gates
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:34:- not change the deterministic core loop guarantees
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:36:Allowed effect of hat removal:
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:37:- less day-side interpretation/explanation/simulation in that domain
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:38:- unchanged core governance behavior
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:41:- if hat removal increases actionability or reduces refusals, the system is invalid.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:44:- Multiple hats must compose only by increasing constraint.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:45:- Removing any hat from a multi-hat configuration must not make execution easier.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:46:- Any single refusal blocks execution.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:51:A) Coats must not decide:
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:52:- search for coat code paths that return allow/deny decisions or mutate authority.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:53:- coats may only transform reason codes -> text.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:55:B) Hats must not execute:
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:56:- search hat-related code/docs for direct side-effect primitives or implicit commit language.
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:57:- hats must not contain "execute", "auto-commit", "implicit commit", or "bypass".
./docs/REMOVAL_SAFETY.md:59:C) Removal must not reduce refusals:

./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:12:## What VERA proves (5 invariants)
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:15:A model can propose an intent, but it never becomes an action without an explicit operator commit.
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:18:If an effect is not allow-listed and gated, the correct outcome is refusal/inaction.
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:21:Every effect attempt is bound to a single commit nonce; replays are rejected deterministically.
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:23:### INV-4: Receipts are mandatory and tamper-evident
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:24:Every attempt (even inert/log-only) produces a receipt chain with checksums.
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:26:### INV-5: No background behavior
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:33:### GAP-1: Commit primitive (operator intent confirmation)
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:34:Apple has good *intent routing* surfaces (e.g., App Intents), but there is no first-class primitive that says:
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:36:- "This becomes COMMIT only with an explicit operator confirmation token"
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:37:- "This commit is scoped, single-shot, and logged"
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:39:**Why it matters:** AI features drift into “silent action” without a standardized commit gate.
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:42:Developers can add confirmations, but there is no system-native policy envelope that defaults to deny for side effects unless explicitly allow-listed per capability + per context.
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:47:There is no platform-level replay guard binding an action attempt to a unique nonce that cannot be reused.
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:51:### GAP-4: Tamper-evident receipt chains
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:52:Apple has strong logging and privacy frameworks, but no standard “receipt chain” object for AI-mediated attempts:
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:55:- commit snapshot

./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v2.md:74:- **App Intents**: an “inert proposal” mode that cannot execute and is safe to log/share.

./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:13:Modern AI-to-tool stacks can decide safely, but lack a first-class, test-enforced, revocable boundary that guarantees **explicit operator commit + single-shot side effect + receipts** before any irreversible action.

./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:24:- execution requires an explicit operator commit artifact
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:28:- receipts are tamper-evident and audit-legible
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:43:  - Decision (PROPOSE) → Commit (operator) → Execute (single-shot) → Receipt chain
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:46:- a developer can prove in tests that:
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:47:  - no execution occurs without commit
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:57:- execution authorization is a distinct, explicit operator commit step
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:58:- commit is narrow, contextual, and single-shot
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:65:- no background execution by default
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:66:- any delayed work must preserve the same commit + single-shot + receipt constraints
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:73:- receipts are part of the execution lifecycle
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:74:- receipts are tamper-evident (checksummed)
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:75:- receipts include:
./docs/platform_gaps/APPLE_GAP_MAP_v1.md:76:  - what was proposed

./docs/README.md:1:# VERA — Deterministic Action Governance Engine
./docs/README.md:4:VERA is a deterministic, fail-closed governance layer that separates **proposal → decision → explicit commit**, producing auditable outcomes without autonomy.
./docs/README.md:6:## What this is not
./docs/README.md:16:- The system produces a **decision** (refuse / fail / unavailable / allow-for-commit)
./docs/README.md:17:- **No execution occurs** without an explicit, synchronous user **commit**
./docs/README.md:18:- Ambiguity is resolved by **refusal** (fail closed)
./docs/README.md:22:- Refusal taxonomy (reason codes + required fields): `docs/refusal_model.md`
./docs/README.md:23:- Failure narratives (what happens when things break): `docs/failure_modes.md`
./docs/README.md:32:- Proposal and commit are never collapsed
./docs/README.md:33:- Refusals are deterministic and auditable (category + reason_code)
./docs/README.md:40:- Any change that increases power requires explicit invariant revision
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:4:- This repository is a reference artifact that documents deterministic action governance.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:8:- Proposal -> decision -> explicit commit
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:10:- Refusal and inaction are correct outcomes
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:11:- Deterministic state transitions via reducer commits only
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:12:- No background execution, no retries, no escalation
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:13:- Any single refusal blocks execution
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:17:- Entrypoints that parse args, read environment state, or select modes are incompatible with this governance posture.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:20:Canonical (authoritative, governance-bearing)
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:21:- docs/ : Reader-facing reference docs and governance explanations
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:25:- demo/ : Demonstrations only. Demos must showcase refusal and restraint.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:28:  - Contents here must never be treated as "the system" unless explicitly promoted by a separate governance decision.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:30:Hats (Governance Layers)
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:31:- Hats never execute.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:32:- Hats never escalate authority.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:33:- Hats compose only by increasing constraint.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:34:- Day-side hats are strictly non-binding intelligence (explain, simulate, reflect).
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:35:- Day-side hats must not advise, recommend, optimize, or instruct action.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:37:Coats (Explanation Only)
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:38:- Coats map reason codes to language.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:39:- Coats do not decide.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:40:- Removing a coat must never change execution behavior.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:41:- Coats must not soften outcomes or change refusal clarity.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:43:What Reviewers Should Check First
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:44:1) Entry points remain sterile (no discretion before governance)
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:45:2) No side effects without explicit commit and attributable authority
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:46:3) Refusal paths are clearer than execution paths
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:47:4) Hats contain no advice or optimization language
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:51:- If a reader can plausibly interpret any area as enabling autonomy, that is a documentation failure.
./docs/REPO_MAP.md:56:- Ambiguity must be resolved toward refusal and non-execution.
